Illinois Tool Works Inc. (the &#8220;Borrower&#8221;) and have represented the Borrower in connection with its execution and delivery of the Amendment Agreement No. 1 to Credit Agreement among the Borrower, ING Bank N.V., London Branch, as Agent, and the Lenders named therein dated as of February 24, 2025 (the &#8220;Amendment&#8221;).   All capitalized terms used in this opinion and not otherwise defined shall have the meanings attributed to them in the Credit Agreement among the Borrower, ING Bank N.V., London Branch, as Agent, and the Lenders named therein dated as of May 5, 2023 (as amended, restated, supplemented or otherwise modified prior to the date hereof and after giving effect to the Amendment, the &#8220;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:111%;text-decoration:underline">Credit Agreement</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:111%">&#8221;).</font></div><div style="text-align:justify;text-indent:36pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:justify;text-indent:36pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">I have examined the Borrower&#8217;s certificate of incorporation, by-laws, resolutions, the Loan Documents (for purposes of this opinion, &#8220;Loan Documents&#8221; shall mean the Credit Agreement, the Amendment and any promissory notes issued thereunder) and such other matters of fact and law which I deem necessary to render this opinion. I have relied on the representations and warranties of the Borrower contained in the Credit Agreement and Amendment with respect to the factual matters set forth therein. Based upon the foregoing, it is my opinion that&#58; </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:justify;text-indent:36pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">1.         The Borrower is validly existing and in good standing under the laws of its state of incorporation and has all requisite authority to conduct its business in each jurisdiction in which its business is conducted, except where the failure to have such authority would not have a Material Adverse Effect. The Borrower has the corporate power and authority to execute and deliver the Amendment. </font></div><div style="text-align:justify;text-indent:36pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:justify;text-indent:36pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">2.         The execution and delivery of the Amendment by the Borrower and the performance by the Borrower of the Obligations have been duly authorized by all necessary corporate action and proceedings on the part of the Borrower and will not&#58; </font></div><div style="text-align:justify;text-indent:36pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:justify;text-indent:72pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">(a)        require any consent of the Borrower&#8217;s shareholders&#59; </font></div><div style="text-align:justify;text-indent:72pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:justify;text-indent:72pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">(b)       violate the Subject Law (as defined below), order, writ, judgment, injunction, decree or award binding on the Borrower or the Borrower&#8217;s amended and restated certificate of incorporation or by-laws or, to my knowledge, any indenture, instrument or agreement binding upon the Borrower&#59; or </font></div><div style="text-align:justify;text-indent:72pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:justify;text-indent:72pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">(c)        result in, or require, the creation or imposition of any Lien pursuant to the provisions of any indenture, instrument or agreement known to me and binding upon the Borrower which could reasonably be expected to have a Material Adverse Effect. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:justify;text-indent:36pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">3.         The Amendment has been duly executed and delivered by the Borrower. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:justify;text-indent:36pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">4. e.removeAttribute('id');a.parentNode.appendChild(e)}}
